## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x23A5 [0x1E] EventEntity looks at LocalPlayer and starts talking
  1: 0x23AA [0x1D] PRINT_EVENT_MESSAGE(message_id=7602*)
     "So what's your friend up to now?\u007F1\u0000\u0007"
  2: 0x23AD [0x23] WAIT_FOR_DIALOG_INTERACTION
  3: 0x23AE [0x1D] PRINT_EVENT_MESSAGE(message_id=7603*)
     "If you don't know, maybe you should find out!\u007F1\u0000\u0007"

  5: 0x23B2 [0x21] END_EVENT
  6: 0x23B3 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
